/*
 * Fix low contrast for Directorist listing email and telephone links.
*/

.directorist-listing-single__info--list a[href^="mailto:"],
.directorist-listing-single__info--list a[href^="tel:"] {

    color: #757575 !important;
    /* Ensure background is white if it's not already */
    /* background-color: #FFFFFF !important; */
}

 * Add consistent hover and focus styles for better user experience and accessibility.
 * This provides visual feedback when interacting with the links.
 */
.directorist-listing-single__info--list a[href^="mailto:"]:hover,
.directorist-listing-single__info--list a[href^="mailto:"]:focus,
.directorist-listing-single__info--list a[href^="tel:"]:hover,
.directorist-listing-single__info--list a[href^="tel:"]:focus {
    color: #0073AA !important; /* A common, accessible link blue for hover/focus */
    text-decoration: underline !important; /* Underline for clear affordance */
}

.directorist-listing-card-text {
    color: #333333 !important; /* A dark grey for excellent contrast */
}

 * Fix low contrast for Directorist pagination numbers.
 */

.directorist-pagination a.page-numbers {
    color: #757575 !important; /* This color meets WCAG AA contrast ratio */
}

 * Ensure hover and focus states also maintain good contrast and provide visual feedback.
 */

.directorist-pagination a.page-numbers:focus {
    color: #0073AA !important; /* A common, accessible link blue for hover/focus */
    text-decoration: underline !important; /* Add underline for better user experience */

		<!-- dce invisible element 3453ec34 -->		<section data-particle_enable="false" data-particle-mobile-disabled="false" class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-59aa667b ugt elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-id="59aa667b" data-element_type="section" data-settings="{&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}">
							<div class="elementor-background-overlay"></div>
							<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-2217d04a" data-id="2217d04a" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-2d15dab1 elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="2d15dab1" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<span class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Upcoming Events</span>				</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-4eb2ebb9 elementor-widget elementor-widget-shortcode" data-id="4eb2ebb9" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="shortcode.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
							<div class="elementor-shortcode"><div id="rst7widget-upcoming-event" class="rst7widget-upcoming-event">
    <div id="rst7widget-events_list" class="rst7widget-events_list">
        <ul>
            <li>Loading data...</li>
        </ul>
    </div>
    <div id="rst7widget-more-event" class="rst7widget-more-event">
        <a href="#" target="_blank"  rel="noopener noreferrer">More Events </a>
    </div>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(document).ready(function () {
        jQuery.get('/asupcomingevents~?t=' + Date.now(), function (data) {
            if (data.code == "200") {
                let events = data.response;
                let is_conference = data.is_conference;
                let show_school_name = data.show_school_name;
                let show_location = data.show_location;

                jQuery('#rst7widget-events_list ul').html('');

                events.map((record) => {
                    let is_away = 0;
                    let line_through = '';
                    let icons = '';
                    if (record.event.indexOf(': ') === -1) {
                        record.event = record.event.replace(':', ': ');
                    }

                    if (record.event.indexOf('Away vs. ')) {
                        if(record.opponent){
                            record.opponent = record.opponent.replace('Away vs. ', '');
                            is_away = 1;
                        }
                    }

                    if (record.status) {
                        if (record.status.indexOf('from') === -1 && (
                            record.status.indexOf('Cancelled') || record.status.indexOf('Rescheduled') ||
                            record.status.indexOf('Postponed') || record.status.indexOf('Date Changed') ||
                            record.status.indexOf('Date & Time Changed')
                        )) {
                            line_through = ' class="line-through"';
                            record.status = ' <span id="red-status" class="red-status">' + record.status + '</span>';
                        }
                    }

                    if (record.online_ticket_url != "" || record.live_video_url != "" || record.live_audio_url != "") {
                        icons += '<object>';

                        if (record.online_ticket_url != "") {
                            icons += '<a href="' + record.online_ticket_url + '" target="_blank"><span id="icon-ticket" class="icon-event" style="font-size:0px;overflow:hidden;">.</span></a>';
                        }

                        if (record.live_video_url != "") {
                            icons += '<a href="' + record.live_video_url + '" target="_blank"><span id="icon-video" class="icon-event" style="font-size:0px;overflow:hidden;">.</span></a>';
                        }

                        if (record.live_audio_url != "") {
                            icons += '<a href="' + record.live_audio_url + '" target="_blank"><span id="icon-sound" class="icon-event" style="font-size:0px;overflow:hidden;">.</span></a>';
                        }

                        icons += '</object><br/>';
                    }

                    if(show_school_name){
                        if(is_conference || is_away){
                            match_data = record.event + ('<br/>' + (record.opponent ? record.opponent + ' vs. ' : '') + record.home);
                        }else{
                            match_data = record.event + ('<br/>' + record.home + (record.opponent ? ' vs. ' + record.opponent : ''));
                        }    
                    }else{
                        match_data = record.event + (record.opponent ? ' vs. ' + record.opponent : '');
                    }

                    jQuery('#rst7widget-events_list ul').append(`
                        <li class="event_item">
                            <a href="${record.permalink}" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">
                                <span ${line_through}>
                                    <strong style="">${record.start_date}</strong><br>
                                    <p class="time_events">
                                        <i class="fa fa-clock-o"></i>${record.start_time}
                                    </p>
                                    ${icons}
                                    ${match_data}
                                    ${(show_location && record.location) ? ('<br/> @ ' + record.location) : ''}
                                </span>
                                ${record.status}
                            </a>
                        </li>
                    `);
                });
                if(data.calendar_url){
                    jQuery('#rst7widget-more-event a').attr('href', data.calendar_url);
                    jQuery('#rst7widget-more-event a').attr("target", "_blank");
                }
            }
        });
    });
</script></div>
						</div>
				</div>

<script id="gpc-modify-link-attributes-js-after">
const addRelAttribute = (element) => {
                if (!element.hasAttribute("href")) return;
                if (!element.hasAttribute("target")) return;

                const targetAttrValue = element.getAttribute("target").trim();
                if (targetAttrValue !== "_blank" && targetAttrValue !== "\"_blank\"") return;

                const relValues = new Set((element.getAttribute("rel") || "").split(" "));
                ["noopener", "noreferrer"].forEach(value => relValues.add(value));

                element.setAttribute("rel", [...relValues].join(" ").trim());
            };

            const processDynamicElement = (element, selector) => {
                if (selector === ".gtranslate_wrapper") {
                    element.addEventListener("pointerenter", () => {
                        setTimeout(() => {
                            element.querySelectorAll("#google_translate_element2 a").forEach(addRelAttribute);
                        }, 500);
                    });
                } else {
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        element.querySelectorAll("a").forEach(addRelAttribute);
                    }, 100);
                }
            };

            const observeSelector = (selector) => {
                const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
                    const element = document.querySelector(selector);
                    if (element) {
                        observer.disconnect();
                        processDynamicElement(element, selector);
                    }
                });

                observer.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });
            };

            const addLinkRelOnJsManipulatedElements = () => {
                const manipulatedElements = [
                    "#pojo-a11y-toolbar",
                    ".gtranslate_wrapper",
                    ".ctf_lightbox_action.ctf_instagram",
                    ".sbi_lightbox_tooltip.sbi_tooltip_social",
                    ".sbi_lightbox_action.sbi_instagram",
                    ".ctf-tweet-text",
                ];

                manipulatedElements.forEach((selector) => {
                    observeSelector(selector);
                });
            };

            const addLinkRelOnElementorWidgets = () => {
                const arrayTargetLinks = [
                    ".sby_video_thumbnail.sby_item_video_thumbnail",
                    ".sby_follow_btn a",
                    "a[href='https://xyzscripts.com/wordpress-plugins/facebook-auto-publish/compare']",
                    "a[href='http://www.xyzscripts.com']",
                    ".ctf-tweet-text a",
                ];
                const targetLinks = document.querySelectorAll(arrayTargetLinks.join(", "));
                
                targetLinks.forEach(elmnt => {
                    addRelAttribute(elmnt);
                });
            }

            document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
                addLinkRelOnJsManipulatedElements();
                addLinkRelOnElementorWidgets();
            });
</script>
